</dd></dl>

<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>

</th>
<td><i>Solo:</i> violin<br /><i>Orchestra:</i> flute, 2 oboes, 2 clarinets, 2 bassoons,<br />2 horns, 2 trumpets, timpani, strings

</th>
